   if(typeof DNT != 'undefined' && DNT==1 &&  DNT_SEEN_COOKIE_STATEMENT != 1 ) {
  document.querySelector('#id_cookie_statement').style.display='block';

function seen_cookie_statement(){
  var d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 30); // valid for 30 days
  document.querySelector('#id_cookie_statement').style.display='none';
  document.cookie = "DNT_SEEN_COOKIE_STATEMENT=1; Path=/; Expires="+d.toUTCString() +";" ;
}
function i_accept(){
  var d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 30); // valid for 30 days
  document.cookie = "DNT=0; Path=/; Expires="+d.toUTCString() +";" ;
  var logger = new Image();
  logger.src = '//analytics.erepublic.com/cms/gdpr/'+btoa(appCore.__persistentData.ef3_contact+';40.77.167.40')+'.gif';
  logger.addEventListener('load', function() {
    location.reload();
  });
}

function learn_more(){
  window.location="https://www.erepublic.com/privacy";
}

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
			var getCookie = function (name) {
				var value = "; " + document.cookie;
				var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
				if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
			};
			// exclude from sections
			var intIsSponsored = $('.article-sponsored').length > 0 ? true : false;
			var intIsResourceModule = $('#rc_dart_ad').length > 0 ? true : false;
			var intIsResourceModule2 = $('.exclude-inarticle').length > 0 ? true : false;

			// eclude from settings in Sitewide Mobile Adhesion Settings
			// billboard settings
			var mobAdhesionExcludeSectionRaw = '/salesforce,/oracle360,/oracle360/*,/smarter,/future,/awsstateandlocal,/salesforce/appexchange,/salesforce/trailblazers,/salesforce/news,/salesforce/papers,/smarter/*,/subscribe/newsletters,/futureofwork,/futureofwork/news,/futureofwork/resources,/futureofwork/conversations';
			var mobAdhesionExcludeContentRaw = '502960651,507225491,512482151,513430371,564990242,566776791, 569925501,571467291,571487811,571838031,571646671,571676851,571664781,571647291,571646671,571572281,571546651,571492041,571487811,571467291,571466731,571450111,571299491,571137751,573900691,573900691';

			window.mobAdhesionSettings = {};
			window.mobAdhesionSettings.excludeSection = mobAdhesionExcludeSectionRaw.split(',');
			window.mobAdhesionSettings.excludeContent = mobAdhesionExcludeContentRaw.split(',');
			//window.mobAdhesionSettings.currentPath = interCurrentPath;
			//window.mobAdhesionSettings.contentId = excludeContentId;
			
			var isMobAdhesionExcluded = window.mobAdhesionSettings.excludeSection.indexOf(interCurrentPath) > -1 ? true : false;
			var isMobAdhesionContentExcluded = window.mobAdhesionSettings.excludeContent.indexOf(excludeContentId) > -1 ? true : false;
			
			// check wildcard subsections
			if( interCurrentPath.indexOf('/') == 0 ){
				var pathParts = interCurrentPath.replace('/', '').split('/');
			} else {
				var pathParts = interCurrentPath.split('/');
			}
			
			// check for subsections
			if( pathParts.length == 2 ){
				var isSubSectionExcluded = window.mobAdhesionSettings.excludeSection.indexOf('/'+pathParts[0]+'/*') > -1 ? true : false;
			}
			
			if( pathParts.length == 3 ){
				var isSubSectionExcluded = window.mobAdhesionSettings.excludeSection.indexOf('/'+pathParts[0]+'/'+pathParts[1]+'/*') > -1 ? true : false;
			}

			// if test, ignore conditions
			if( window.location.search.indexOf('moad=1') == -1 ){

				//console.log("DFP: 4.0 - Check if mobile device: " +isMobileDevice() );
				if( !isMobileDevice() ){
					//console.log('NOT a mobile device, Mobile_Adhesion will not be displayed.');
					$('#mobAdB').remove();
				}

				//console.log("DFP: 4.1 - Check exclude section.");
				if( isSubSectionExcluded ){
					//console.log('Mobile_Adhesion is excluded from sub section per Sitewide Settings [493635451]');
					$('#mobAdB').remove();
				}

				//console.log("DFP: 4.2 - Check exclude section #2.");
				if( isMobAdhesionExcluded || isMobAdhesionContentExcluded ){
					//console.log('Mobile_Adhesion is excluded from this section per Sitewide Settings [493635451]');
					$('#mobAdB').remove();
				}
				
				//console.log("DFP: 4.3 - Check exclude from sponsored.");
				if( intIsSponsored ){
					//console.log('Sponsored, removing Mobile_Adhesion');
					$('#mobAdB').remove();
				}

				//console.log("DFP: 4.4 - Check exclude from RS module.");
				/* RULE REMOVED per Adam & Zach
				if( intIsResourceModule || intIsResourceModule2 ){
					//console.log('Resource Module detected, removing Mobile_Adhesion');
					$('#mobAdB').remove();
				}
				*/

				// remove if homepage for testing new mobile
				/*
				if( window.location.pathname == "/" ){
					//console.log('Homepage not showing Mobile_Adhesion');
					$('#mobAdB').remove();
				}
				*/

				// Get Mobile_Adhesion cookie
				var mobAdcookieVal = getCookie( 'mobAdCookie' ); // return Boolean

				//console.log("DFP: 4.5 - Check cookie if seen: " + (mobAdcookieVal !== undefined ? "seen" : "NOT seen"));
				if( mobAdcookieVal !== undefined ){
					//console.log('Mobile_Adhesion HAS BEEN seen. mobAdCookie is set');
					//$('#mobAdB').remove(); // show ad everytime, even when user closes mobile adhesion @11-05-2020
				}

			}

			// load ads if '#mobAdB' isnt removed
			
			if( $('#mobAdB').length != 0 ){
				$('#mobAdB').removeClass('hidden');
				// call ad 
				//console.log("DFP: 5 - Do ad call.");
				googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('mob-adhesion-slot'); });
				$('.closeMobAdBtnDiv').removeClass('hidden');
			}
			
			$('#mobAdB').on('click', '.closeMobAdBtn', function(e){
				e.preventDefault();
				//console.log('Closing MobAd');
				$('#mobAdB').addClass('hidden');
				$('#mobAdB').remove();
				$('#mobAdB').removeClass('visible-xs');

				var d1 = new Date();
				var expireDate = new Date ( d1 );
				expireDate.setMinutes ( d1.getMinutes() + 20 ); // 20 minutes
				var expiresTemp = "expires="+ expireDate.toUTCString();
				document.cookie = "mobAdCookie=true;" + expiresTemp + ";path=/";
			});
		});
  </script>
